#Buyer
<!-- START_d8aed1ca8ee6d1bf42f4f45d688f33db -->
## Display a listing of the resource.

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X GET "http://bangsinibang.dev/buyers" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://bangsinibang.dev/buyers",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

## Display the specified resource.

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X GET "http://bangsinibang.dev/buyers/{buyer}" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://bangsinibang.dev/buyers/{buyer}",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

> Example response:

```json
{
    "error": "Your buyer does not exist with specified identificator",
    "code": 404
}
```

## Display the specified resource.

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X GET "http://bangsinibang.dev/categories/{category}" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://bangsinibang.dev/categories/{category}",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

> Example response:

```json
{
    "error": "Your category does not exist with specified identificator",
    "code": 404
}
```

## Store a newly created resource in storage.

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X POST "http://bangsinibang.dev/favorites" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://bangsinibang.dev/favorites",
    "method": "POST",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```


### HTTP Request
`POST favorites`


<!-- END_b4d32a9ad1af96835ae3c15fbd0d1170 -->

<!-- START_684b25d29f846086f9768a99288c2d7b -->
## Display the specified resource.

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X GET "http://bangsinibang.dev/favorites/{favorite}" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://bangsinibang.dev/favorites/{favorite}",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

> Example response:

```json
{
    "error": "Your favorite does not exist with specified identificator",
    "code": 404
}
```

#Main Service

```bash
curl -X GET "http://bangsinibang.dev/mainservices" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://bangsinibang.dev/mainservices",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
```

## Display the specified resource.

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X GET "http://bangsinibang.dev/mainservices/{mainservice}" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://bangsinibang.dev/mainservices/{mainservice}",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

> Example response:

```json
{
    "error": "Your mainservice does not exist with specified identificator",
    "code": 404
}
```

## Store a newly created resource in storage.

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X POST "http://bangsinibang.dev/transactions" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://bangsinibang.dev/transactions",
    "method": "POST",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

## Display the specified resource.

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X GET "http://bangsinibang.dev/transactions/{transaction}" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://bangsinibang.dev/transactions/{transaction}",
    "method": "GET",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```

> Example response:

```json
{
    "error": "Your transaction does not exist with specified identificator",
    "code": 404
}
```

```bash
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {

    "crossDomain": true,
```

## Store a newly created resource in storage.

> Example request:

```bash
curl -X POST "http://bangsinibang.dev/users" \
-H "Accept: application/json"
```

```javascript
var settings = {
    "async": true,
    "crossDomain": true,
    "url": "http://bangsinibang.dev/users",
    "method": "POST",
    "headers": {
        "accept": "application/json"
    }
}

$.ajax(settings).done(function (response) {
    console.log(response);
});
```


### HTTP Request
`POST users`


<!-- END_57a8a4ba671355511e22780b1b63690e -->
